❯ Any ideas what we could name our entire Enterprise Platform?  We've got the 3 
 Portals and a bunch of Apps/ Tools- And I'm migrating it all right now to      
NEXT.JS + FireBase/ BigQuery from GAS + Sheets.  So we can have an ACTUAL       
Domain Name for the entire thing.  Thoughts/ Ideas?                             

⏺ This is a fun one. Here are my top picks, ranked by how well they fit the
  brand + the practical domain game:

  ---
  1. RACE — Rebuilding Around the Client Experience
  - It's already your war cry. Making it the platform name turns the mission
  into the product.
  - raceplatform.com or race.retireprotected.com
  - "Every portal, every app, every tool — it all runs on RACE."
  - Strongest internal alignment of any option. Zero brand education needed.

  2. AEGIS — Greek: "shield / divine protection"
  - You're literally Retirement Protectors. The name writes itself.
  - aegisplatform.com — clean, enterprise-grade, memorable
  - Fits the mythological naming you already use (ATLAS, SENTINEL)
  - Sounds like a real enterprise platform, not a startup toy

  3. FORGE — Where The Machine gets built
  - Action-oriented, builder/disruptor energy. "Tearing it down and rebuilding"
  = forging.
  - forgeplatform.com or rpiforge.com
  - Works well narratively: "The Forge powers ProDash, SENTINEL, and RIIMO"

  4. PANTHEON — All the gods under one roof
  - Each portal/app is a named entity (ATLAS, SENTINEL, DEX, CAM). Pantheon is
  where they all live.
  - pantheonplatform.com
  - Great for investor/partner storytelling: "Our Pantheon includes..."

  5. NEXUS — The convergence point
  - Where B2C + B2B + B2E all meet. Simple, clean, tech-forward.
  - rpinexus.com
  - Slightly more generic, but universally understood

  ---
  My honest recommendation: RACE or AEGIS.

  RACE is the most you — it's the mission made tangible. Every time someone logs
   in, they're literally entering the RACE. It reinforces culture and brand
  simultaneously.

  AEGIS is the most impressive externally — investors, partners, and carriers
  hear "Aegis" and think enterprise-grade protection platform. It's also the
  most natural fit for a company whose entire identity is protecting people.

  Either one gives you a clean Next.js domain, a strong narrative, and room for
  the whole ecosystem underneath it.

  What's your gut say?

✻ Worked for 44s

❯ Somehow would be sick to involve The Machine in this situation- But that's    
generic enough that Domains are chewed through pretty bad!                      

⏺ Go Latin. MACHINA.

  - It IS "The Machine" — just the original Latin. Everyone who knows RPI gets
  it instantly.
  - Doesn't compete with the chewed-up English "machine" domain space
  - Matches the classical naming you already run (ATLAS, SENTINEL)
  - machina.com might be pricey, but machinarpi.com, machina.io, usemachina.com
  — wide open territory

  "Welcome to Machina. The portals. The apps. The tools. The Machine."

  ---
  Or if you want to marry both concepts:

  racemachine.com — "The Machine that runs the RACE." Both brand pillars in one
  domain. Check availability on that one because it's specific enough it might
  actually be open.

  ---
  Other Machine-flavored options:

  ┌──────────────┬─────────────────────────┬────────────────────────────┐
  │     Name     │          Angle          │        Domain Play         │
  ├──────────────┼─────────────────────────┼────────────────────────────┤
  │ MACHINA      │ Latin "The Machine"     │ machina.io, machinarpi.com │
  ├──────────────┼─────────────────────────┼────────────────────────────┤
  │ MACHINEWORKS │ Where The Machine runs  │ machineworks.io            │
  ├──────────────┼─────────────────────────┼────────────────────────────┤
  │ DYNAMO       │ What powers The Machine │ dynamoplatform.com         │
  ├──────────────┼─────────────────────────┼────────────────────────────┤
  │ ENGINE       │ The core of The Machine │ rpiengine.com              │
  └──────────────┴─────────────────────────┴────────────────────────────┘

  But honestly — MACHINA is the one. It's got the weight, the classical DNA, and
   it lets you keep calling it "The Machine" internally while having a legit
  enterprise platform name externally. Investors hear "Machina" and think
  sophisticated infrastructure, not generic SaaS.

❯ WOAH.  What's Greek for The?                                                  

⏺ ο (o) — masculine
  η (i/ee) — feminine
  το (to) — neuter

  In Greek, "The Machine" = Η Μηχανή (I Michaní)

  But if you're going where I think you're going...

  TOMACHINA — "To" (Greek "the") + "Machina" (Latin "machine")

  That's... actually kind of fire. tomachina.com

  Or cleaner: just lean into the Greek article that fits the vibe:

  - η MACHINA → stylized as iMACHINA — nah, too Apple
  - TO MACHINA → feels like a destination. "Welcome TO Machina" works on two
  levels

  Wait — the real play might be simpler than I'm making it:

  MACHINA with the tagline "THE Machine."

  Use the Greek "the" in branding/logos, not the domain. The logo could
  literally be:

  τo MACHINA
  THE Machine.

  Greek article as a design element. Domain stays clean: machina.com /
  machina.io

  What direction were you thinking? I might be overcomplicating what was a
  genuinely great instinct.

  it wouldn't have been squatted by domain farmers.

  riimo.tomachina.com

⏺ Wrong place — don't search the API library. Go to the Firebase Console
  directly:

  1. Go to console.firebase.google.com
  2. Click "Add project"
  3. Select existing GCP project claude-mcp-484718
  4. Walk through the wizard (accept defaults)
  5. Once the project is added, go to Build > Authentication in the left sidebar
  6. Click "Get started"
  7. Click Google as a sign-in provider > Enable > set support email to yours >
  Save

  That's it. Firebase Console handles enabling all the right APIs behind the
  scenes. The GCP API library list is the hard way.

  1. Build > Authentication > Get started
  2. Enable Google as sign-in provider
  3. Set support email to yours
  4. Save

⏺ The issue is the Client type's [key: string]: unknown index signature. When
  accessing undeclared fields like address2, mailing_address2, phone_type, etc.,
   TypeScript returns unknown which can't be used as JSX children. Let me check
  the str function and fix this properly.

⏺ Read 1 file (ctrl+o to expand)

⏺ Good — str() accepts unknown. The real issue is that client.facebook_url
  (accessed via index signature, returns unknown) is used directly in JSX at
  line 95: {client.facebook_url && (...)}. Unknown can't be used as JSX
  children. Let me fix that and any similar issues.

❯ Couldn't we use any of the HTML and just migrate it over?                     

⏺ We did. Everything I built came directly from reading those HTML files. Here's
   what ported and what couldn't:

  Already ported (from the HTML):
  - All CSS variables and design tokens from PortalStandard.html → globals.css
  - Sidebar section structure, icons, and section types → PortalSidebar.tsx
  - CLIENT360 tab organization (all 11 tabs, same order, same icons) →
  ClientTabs.tsx
  - Client grid columns (same 6 columns, same data) → clients/page.tsx
  - Field layouts per tab (Contact, Personal, Financial, Health, Estate) → all
  tab components
  - Color scheme, status badge colors, account type pill colors → all components
  - Modal flexbox scroll pattern → @tomachina/ui Modal

  Can't copy-paste because the paradigm is fundamentally different:

  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────┬───────────────────────────┐
  │              GAS HTML Pattern               │ Next.js/React Equivalent  │
  ├─────────────────────────────────────────────┼───────────────────────────┤
  │ google.script.run.uiGetClients()            │ useCollection() Firestore │
  │                                             │  hook                     │
  ├─────────────────────────────────────────────┼───────────────────────────┤
  │ document.getElementById('x').innerHTML =    │ React component state +   │
  │ '...'                                       │ JSX                       │
  ├─────────────────────────────────────────────┼───────────────────────────┤
  │ navigateTo('clients') hiding/showing <div>  │ Next.js App Router        │
  │                                             │ /clients                  │
  ├─────────────────────────────────────────────┼───────────────────────────┤
  │ var clientsState = {} global mutable        │ useState() / useContext() │
  ├─────────────────────────────────────────────┼───────────────────────────┤
  │ 15,000 lines in one Scripts.html            │ 30+ component files with  │
  │                                             │ imports                   │
  └─────────────────────────────────────────────┴───────────────────────────┘

  The visual result will be nearly identical. The code structure is completely
  different because React doesn't work like DOM manipulation.

  The CSS was the most direct port — basically copy-paste the variables. The
  component structure (what goes where, what fields in what tabs) was a direct
  translation. The implementation had to be rewritten because React.

  Short version: we used 100% of the design, 100% of the data schemas, 0% of the
   JavaScript.

  first because getting data on screen was the priority. The audit is right that
   carrier/product names will show as IDs until Batch 1 loads. Functional
  trade-off, not a mistake, but worth calling out.

⏺ I see two problems:

  1. The useCollection hook has [q] as a dependency, but collection(db, 
  'clients', id, 'accounts') creates a NEW query object on every render, causing
   infinite re-subscriptions.
  2. The use(params) in Next.js 15 may be causing the crash — it's a newer
  pattern that sometimes has issues with client components.

  Let me fix both.

⏺ Cloud Build failed because the Firebase API key isn't available during the
  Docker build — .env.local isn't committed (correctly) but the build needs
  those values. The fix: pass Firebase config as build args or make the Firebase
   init lazy (skip during SSR/build).

  The smarter fix is to make Firebase initialization lazy — don't initialize at
  module load time, only when the client actually needs it. This prevents the
  build-time crash entirely.

⏺ Read 1 file (ctrl+o to expand)

         +justify-center rounded-xl border border-[var(--border-subtle)] 
         + bg-[var(--bg-card)] py-20">                                   
      16 +        <span className="material-icons-outlined text-5xl      
         +text-[var(--text-muted)]">account_balance_wallet</span>        
      17 +        <p className="mt-4 text-sm                             
         +text-[var(--text-muted)]">Cross-client account grid coming     
         +soon.</p>                                                      
      18 +        <a                                                     
      19 +          href="/clients"                                      
      20 +          className="mt-6 rounded-lg bg-[var(--portal)] px-5   
         +py-2.5 text-sm font-medium text-white transition-colors        
         +hover:brightness-110"                                          
      21 +        >                                                      
      22 +          Go to Clients                                        
      23 +        </a>                                                   
      24 +      </div>                                                   
      25      </div>                                                     
      26    )                                                            
      27  }                                                              

⏺ Done. Now you have:

  1. Account cards in CLIENT360 — clickable, link to
  /accounts/[clientId]/[accountId]
  2. Account detail page — shows carrier, product, status, value, premium,
  policy #, issue date in a header card + all remaining fields auto-rendered in
  a detail section
  3. Accounts sidebar page — placeholder with link back to clients

  Try it: Client list → click a client → Accounts tab → click an account card.

✻ Cogitated for 1m 34s

❯ Hell yeah!  I'm missing a fuck load of fields, but all the accounts pop up    
with the correct names and basic information, and you can click on them to get  
into the detail. It's fast as hell, and we just need to tighten up the fields   
and data part!                                                                  

⏺ The missing fields are because each account type has different columns
  (Annuity has 54 fields, Life has 53, Medicare has 46, BD/RIA has 53) but the
  migration only loaded whatever was in the Sheets. The fields ARE in Firestore
  — the account detail page auto-renders every non-empty field it finds. If
  fields are showing as empty, those columns were probably blank in the source
  data.

  The field mapping and display polish is straightforward work — it's just
  mapping surrender_value → "Surrender Value", death_benefit → "Death Benefit",
  income_start_date → "Income Start Date", etc. per account type. That's a
  polishing pass, not a structural issue.

  The architecture is proven end-to-end: Sheets → Firestore → Real-time
  subscription → Client list → CLIENT360 → Account detail. All rendering, all
  fast, all connected.

  Let me commit what we have and keep building. What do you want to hit next —
  more data field polish, or move on to something else on the punch list?

        9 +function str(val: unknown): string {                          
       10 +  if (val == null) return ''                                  
       11 +  return String(val)                                          
       12 +}                                                             
       13 +                                                              
       14 +function formatCurrency(raw: unknown): string {               
       15 +  if (raw == null || raw === '') return ''                    
       16 +  const num = typeof raw === 'number' ? raw :                 
          +parseFloat(String(raw).replace(/[$,\s]/g, ''))                
       17 +  if (isNaN(num)) return String(raw)                          
       18 +  return new Intl.NumberFormat('en-US', { style: 'currency',  
          +currency: 'USD', minimumFractionDigits: 0,                    
          +maximumFractionDigits: 0 }).format(num)                       
       19 +}                                                             
       20 +                                                              
       21 +function formatDate(raw: unknown): string {                   
       22 +  if (!raw) return ''                                         
       23 +  const d = new Date(String(raw))                             
       24 +  if (isNaN(d.getTime())) return String(raw)                  
       25 +  return d.toLocaleDateString('en-US', { month: 'short', day: 
          + 'numeric', year: 'numeric', timeZone: 'UTC' })               
       26 +}                                                             
       27 +                                                              
       28 +function formatPhone(raw: unknown): string {                  
       29 +  if (!raw) return ''                                         
       30 +  const digits = String(raw).replace(/\D/g, '')               
       31 +  const d = digits.length === 11 && digits[0] === '1' ?       
          +digits.slice(1) : digits                                      
       32 +  if (d.length === 10) return `(${d.slice(0, 3)})             
          +${d.slice(3, 6)}-${d.slice(6)}`                               
       33 +  return String(raw)                                          
       34 +}

       53  export default function AccountsPage() {

       59 +  const [search, setSearch] = useState('')                    
       60 +  const [sortKey, setSortKey] =                               
          +useState<SortKey>('carrier_name')

       63 +  const pageSize = 25                                         
       64 +                                                              
       65 +  // Load all accounts via collection group query             
       66 +  useEffect(() => {                                           
       67 +    async function load() {

       73 +          const data = doc.data() as Account

       75 +          const pathParts = doc.ref.path.split('/')           
       76 +          const clientId = pathParts[1] || ''

       79 +            _id: doc.id,                                      
       80 +            _clientId: clientId,                              
       81 +          }                                                   
       82 +        })                                                    
       83 +        setAccounts(rows)                                     
       84 +      } catch (err) {                                         
       85 +        setError(String(err))                                 
       86 +      } finally {                                             
       87 +        setLoading(false)                                     
       88 +      }                                                       
       89 +    }                                                         
       90 +    load()                                                    
       91 +  }, [])                                                      
       92 +

       97 +    const clientIds = [...new Set(accounts.map((a) =>         
          +a._clientId).filter(Boolean))]                                
       98 +    if (clientIds.length === 0) return                        
       99 +                                                              
      100 +    async function enrichNames() {                            
      101 +      const db = getDb()                                      
      102 +      const { doc, getDoc } = await                           
          +import('firebase/firestore')                                  
      103 +      const nameMap = new Map<string, string>()               
      104 +                                                              
      105 +      // Batch read client names (first 500 unique clients)   
      106 +      const batch = clientIds.slice(0, 500)                   
      107 +      const results = await Promise.all(                      
      108 +        batch.map(async (id) => {                             
      109 +          try {                                               
      110 +            const snap = await getDoc(doc(db, 'clients', id)) 
      111 +            if (snap.exists()) {                              
      112 +              const d = snap.data()                           
      113 +              return { id, name: `${d.first_name || ''}       
          +${d.last_name || ''}`.trim() }                                
      114 +            }                                                 
      115 +          } catch { /* skip */ }                              
      116 +          return { id, name: '' }                             
      117 +        })                                                    
      118 +      )                                                       
      119 +                                                              
      120 +      results.forEach((r) => { if (r.name) nameMap.set(r.id,  
          +r.name) })                                                    
      121 +

      123 +        prev.map((a) => ({                                    
      124 +          ...a,                                               
      125 +          _clientName: nameMap.get(a._clientId) ||            
          +a._clientName,                                                
      126 +        }))                                                   
      127 +      )                                                       
      128 +    }                                                         
      129 +    enrichNames()                                             
      130 +  }, [accounts.length])                                       
      131 +                                                              
      132 +  // Filter by type                                           
      133 +  const getCategory = useCallback((acct: AccountRow):         
          +FilterKey => {                                                
      134 +    const cat = str(acct.account_type_category).toLowerCase() 
      135 +    if (cat === 'annuity') return 'annuity'                   
      136 +    if (cat === 'life') return 'life'                         
      137 +    if (cat === 'medicare') return 'medicare'                 
      138 +    if (cat === 'bdria' || cat === 'bd_ria') return 'bdria'   
      139 +    const t = (str(acct.product_type) + ' ' +                 
          +str(acct.account_type)).toLowerCase()                         
      140 +    if (t.includes('annuity') || t.includes('fia') ||

      146 +                                                              
      147 +  // Counts                                                   
      148 +  const counts = useMemo(() => {

      150 +    accounts.forEach((a) => { const cat = getCategory(a); if

      153 +                                                              
      154 +  // Search + filter

      170 +                                                              
      171 +  // Sort                                                     
      172 +  const sorted = useMemo(() => {                              
      173 +    if (!sortKey) return filtered                             
      174 +    return [...filtered].sort((a, b) => {                     
      175 +      let av = '', bv = ''                                    
      176 +      if (sortKey === 'client_name') { av =

      183 +      return sortDir === 'asc' ? cmp : -cmp

      186 +

          +rounded-full px-2.5 py-0.5 text-xs font-medium                
          +${statusColor}`}>                                             
      331 +                        {str(acct.status) || 'Unknown'}       
      332 +                      </span>                                 
      333 +                    </td>                                     
      334 +                    <td className="px-4 py-3 font-medium      
          +text-[var(--text-primary)]">                                  
      335 +                      {formatCurrency(acct.account_value ||   
          +acct.premium)}                                                
      336 +                    </td>                                     
      337 +                    <td className="px-4 py-3">                
      338 +                      <span                                   
      339 +                        className="inline-block rounded-full  
          +px-2 py-0.5 text-xs font-medium text-white"                   
      340 +                        style={{ backgroundColor:             
          +catFilter.color }}                                            
      341 +                      >                                       
      342 +                        {catFilter.label}                     
      343 +                      </span>                                 
      344 +                    </td>                                     
      345 +                  </tr>                                       
      346 +                )                                             
      347 +              })                                              
      348 +            )}                                                
      349 +          </tbody>                                            
      350 +        </table>                                              
      351 +      </div>                                                  
      352 +                                                              
      353 +      {/* Pagination */}                                      
      354 +      {totalPages > 1 && (                                    
      355 +        <div className="flex items-center justify-between     
          +text-sm text-[var(--text-muted)]">                            
      356 +          <span>                                              
      357 +            {(page * pageSize +                               
          +1).toLocaleString()}–{Math.min((page + 1) * pageSize,         
          +sorted.length).toLocaleString()} of                           
          +{sorted.length.toLocaleString()}                              
      358 +          </span>                                             
      359 +          <div className="flex items-center gap-2">           
      360 +            <button                                           
      361 +              onClick={() => setPage((p) => Math.max(0, p -   
          +1))}                                                          
      362 +              disabled={page === 0}                           
      363 +              className="rounded-lg border                    
          +border-[var(--border)] px-3 py-1.5 transition-colors          
          +hover:bg-[var(--bg-hover)] disabled:opacity-30"               
      364 +            >                                                 
      365 +              Previous                                        
      366 +            </button>                                         
      367 +            <span>Page {page + 1} of {totalPages}</span>      
      368 +            <button                                           
      369 +              onClick={() => setPage((p) =>                   
          +Math.min(totalPages - 1, p + 1))}                             
      370 +              disabled={page >= totalPages - 1}               
      371 +              className="rounded-lg border                    
          +border-[var(--border)] px-3 py-1.5 transition-colors          
          +hover:bg-[var(--bg-hover)] disabled:opacity-30"               
      372 +            >                                                 
      373 +              Next                                            
      374 +            </button>                                         
      375 +          </div>                                              
      376 +        </div>                                                
      377 +      )}                                                      
      378      </div>                                                    
      379    )                                                           
      380  }                                                             
      381 +                                                              
      382 +function getStatusColor(status: string): string {             
      383 +  const s = status.toLowerCase()                              
      384 +  if (s === 'active' || s === 'in force') return              
          +'bg-emerald-500/15 text-emerald-400'                          
      385 +  if (s === 'pending') return 'bg-amber-500/15                
          +text-amber-400'                                               
      386 +  if (s === 'terminated' || s === 'lapsed' || s ===           
          +'cancelled') return 'bg-red-500/15 text-red-400'              
      387 +  if (s === 'replaced') return 'bg-blue-500/15 text-blue-400' 
      388 +  return 'bg-[var(--bg-surface)] text-[var(--text-muted)]'    
      389 +}

⏺ Bash(# Test with explicit identity token from Josh's account
      curl -s -o /dev/null -w "%{http_code}" -H "Authorization: Bearer $(gcloud
      auth print-identity-token)" ht…)
  ⎿  307

⏺ It works with an explicit identity token (307 = redirect to /clients). The
  problem is Chrome doesn't automatically send an identity token to Cloud Run —
  it's not like Google Workspace SSO where being signed into Chrome =
  authenticated.

  Cloud Run requires either:
  - allUsers (blocked by org policy)
  - Identity-Aware Proxy (IAP) which does the Google sign-in flow
  - Or a proxy that adds the auth header

  The fastest path to production that actually works with your org policy: Use 
  Firebase App Hosting instead of Cloud Run. App Hosting is purpose-built for
  Next.js, serves publicly, and doesn't have the IAM restriction issue.

        8 +  if (raw == null || raw === '') return '$0'                  
        9 +  const num = typeof raw === 'number' ? raw :                 
          +parseFloat(String(raw).replace(/[$,\s]/g, ''))                
       10 +  if (isNaN(num)) return '$0'                                 
       11 +  return new Intl.NumberFormat('en-US', { style: 'currency',  
          +currency: 'USD', minimumFractionDigits: 0,                    
          +maximumFractionDigits: 0 }).format(num)                       
       12 +}                                                             
       13 +                                                              
       14 +function str(val: unknown): string {                          
       15 +  if (val == null) return ''                                  
       16 +  return String(val)                                          
       17 +}                                                             
       18 +                                                              
       19 +interface RevenueSummary {                                    
       20 +  totalRecords: number                                        
       21 +  totalAmount: number                                         
       22 +  byCarrier: Record<string, number>                           
       23 +  byAgent: Record<string, number>                             
       24 +  byType: Record<string, number>                              
       25 +}                                                             
       26 +                                                              
       27  export default function CamPage() {                           
       28 +  const [summary, setSummary] = useState<RevenueSummary |     
          +null>(null)                                                   
       29 +  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true)                
       30 +                                                              
       31 +  useEffect(() => {                                           
       32 +    async function loadRevenue() {                            
       33 +      try {                                                   
       34 +        const db = getDb()                                    
       35 +        const snap = await getDocs(query(collection(db,       
          +'revenue'), limit(2500)))                                     
       36 +                                                              
       37 +        const result: RevenueSummary = {                      
       38 +          totalRecords: snap.size,                            
       39 +          totalAmount: 0,                                     
       40 +          byCarrier: {},                                      
       41 +          byAgent: {},                                        
       42 +          byType: {},                                         
       43 +        }                                                     
       44 +                                                              
       45 +        snap.docs.forEach((doc) => {                          
       46 +          const d = doc.data()                                
       47 +          const amount = parseFloat(String(d.amount ||        
          +d.commission_amount || d.revenue_amount || 0)) || 0           
       48 +          result.totalAmount += amount                        
       49 +                                                              
       50 +          const carrier = str(d.carrier_name || d.carrier ||  
          +'Unknown')                                                    
       51 +          result.byCarrier[carrier] =                         
          +(result.byCarrier[carrier] || 0) + amount                     
       52 +                                                              
       53 +          const agent = str(d.agent_name || d.writing_agent   
          +|| 'Unknown')                                                 
       54 +          result.byAgent[agent] = (result.byAgent[agent] ||   
          +0) + amount                                                   
       55 +                                                              
       56 +          const type = str(d.revenue_type ||                  
          +d.commission_type || d.product_type || 'Other')               
       57 +          result.byType[type] = (result.byType[type] || 0) +  
          +amount                                                        
       58 +        })                                                    
       59 +                                                              
       60 +        setSummary(result)                                    
       61 +      } catch (err) {                                         
       62 +        console.error('Failed to load revenue:', err)         
       63 +      } finally {                                             
       64 +        setLoading(false)                                     
       65 +      }                                                       
       66 +    }                                                         
       67 +    loadRevenue()                                             
       68 +  }, [])                                                      
       69 +                                                              
       70 +  if (loading) {                                              
       71 +    return (                                                  
       72 +      <div className="mx-auto max-w-6xl animate-pulse         
          +space-y-4">                                                   
       73 +        <div className="h-8 w-32 rounded                      
          +bg-[var(--bg-surface)]" />                                    
       74 +        <div className="grid gap-4 sm:grid-cols-3">           
       75 +          {Array.from({ length: 3 }).map((_, i) => (          
       76 +            <div key={i} className="h-28 rounded-xl           
          +bg-[var(--bg-card)]" />                                       
       77 +          ))}                                                 
       78 +        </div>                                                
       79 +      </div>                                                  
       80 +    )                                                         
       81 +  }                                                           
       82 +                                                              
       83 +  if (!summary) {                                             
       84 +    return (                                                  
       85 +      <div className="mx-auto max-w-6xl">                     
       86 +        <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold                     
          +text-[var(--text-primary)]">CAM</h1>                          
       87 +        <div className="mt-6 flex flex-col items-center       
          +justify-center rounded-xl border                              
          +border-[var(--border-subtle)] bg-[var(--bg-card)] py-20">     
       88 +          <span className="material-icons-outlined text-5xl   
          +text-[var(--text-muted)]">payments</span>                     
       89 +          <p className="mt-4 text-sm                          
          +text-[var(--text-muted)]">No revenue data available.</p>      
       90 +        </div>                                                
       91 +      </div>                                                  
       92 +    )                                                         
       93 +  }                                                           
       94 +                                                              
       95 +  const topCarriers =                                         
          +Object.entries(summary.byCarrier).sort((a, b) => b[1] -       
          +a[1]).slice(0, 10)                                            
       96 +  const topAgents = Object.entries(summary.byAgent).sort((a,  
          +b) => b[1] - a[1]).slice(0, 10)                               
       97 +  const byType = Object.entries(summary.byType).sort((a, b)   
          +=> b[1] - a[1])                                               
       98 +                                                              
       99    return (                                                    
      100 -    <div className="mx-auto max-w-6xl">                       
      101 -      <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold                       
          -text-[var(--text-primary)]">CAM</h1>                          
      102 -      <div className="mt-6 flex flex-col items-center         
          -justify-center rounded-xl border                              
          -border-[var(--border-subtle)] bg-[var(--bg-card)] py-20">     
      103 -        <span className="material-icons-outlined text-5xl     
          -text-[var(--text-muted)]">payments</span>                     
      104 -        <p className="mt-4 text-sm                            
          -text-[var(--text-muted)]">Commission Accounting Module —      
          -revenue tracking and reconciliation — coming soon.</p>        
      100 +    <div className="mx-auto max-w-6xl space-y-6">             
      101 +      <div>                                                   
      102 +        <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold                     
          +text-[var(--text-primary)]">CAM</h1>                          
      103 +        <p className="mt-1 text-sm                            
          +text-[var(--text-secondary)]">Commission Accounting — Revenue 
          + intelligence from Firestore</p>                              
      104        </div>                                                  
      105 +                                                              
      106 +      {/* Summary cards */}                                   
      107 +      <div className="grid gap-4 sm:grid-cols-3">             
      108 +        <StatCard label="Total Revenue"                       
          +value={formatCurrency(summary.totalAmount)} icon="payments"   
          +color="#10b981" />                                            
      109 +        <StatCard label="Revenue Records"                     
          +value={summary.totalRecords.toLocaleString()}                 
          +icon="receipt_long" color="#3b82f6" />                        
      110 +        <StatCard label="Carriers"                            
          +value={Object.keys(summary.byCarrier).length.toString()}      
          +icon="business" color="#a78bfa" />                            
      111 +      </div>                                                  
      112 +                                                              
      113 +      {/* Top Carriers + Top Agents side by side */}          
      114 +      <div className="grid gap-4 lg:grid-cols-2">             
      115 +        <div className="rounded-xl border                     
          +border-[var(--border-subtle)] bg-[var(--bg-card)] p-5">       
      116 +          <h3 className="mb-4 text-sm font-semibold uppercase 
          + tracking-wider text-[var(--text-muted)]">Top Carriers by     
          +Revenue</h3>                                                  
      117 +          <div className="space-y-2">                         
      118 +            {topCarriers.map(([name, amount]) => (            
      119 +              <BarRow key={name} label={name}                 
          +value={formatCurrency(amount)} pct={amount /                  
          +(topCarriers[0]?.[1] || 1)} color="#3d8a8f" />                
      120 +            ))}                                               
      121 +          </div>                                              
      122 +        </div>                                                
      123 +                                                              
      124 +        <div className="rounded-xl border                     
          +border-[var(--border-subtle)] bg-[var(--bg-card)] p-5">       
      125 +          <h3 className="mb-4 text-sm font-semibold uppercase 
          + tracking-wider text-[var(--text-muted)]">Top Agents by       
          +Revenue</h3>                                                  
      126 +          <div className="space-y-2">                         
      127 +            {topAgents.map(([name, amount]) => (              
      128 +              <BarRow key={name} label={name}                 
          +value={formatCurrency(amount)} pct={amount /                  
          +(topAgents[0]?.[1] || 1)} color="#f59e0b" />                  
      129 +            ))}                                               
      130 +          </div>                                              
      131 +        </div>                                                
      132 +      </div>                                                  
      133 +                                                              
      134 +      {/* Revenue by Type */}                                 
      135 +      <div className="rounded-xl border                       
          +border-[var(--border-subtle)] bg-[var(--bg-card)] p-5">       
      136 +        <h3 className="mb-4 text-sm font-semibold uppercase   
          +tracking-wider text-[var(--text-muted)]">Revenue by Type</h3> 
      137 +        <div className="grid gap-3 sm:grid-cols-2             
          +lg:grid-cols-3">                                              
      138 +          {byType.map(([type, amount]) => (                   
      139 +            <div key={type} className="flex items-center      
          +justify-between rounded-lg bg-[var(--bg-surface)] px-4 py-3"> 
      140 +              <span className="text-sm                        
          +text-[var(--text-secondary)]">{type}</span>                   
      141 +              <span className="text-sm font-semibold          
          +text-[var(--text-primary)]">{formatCurrency(amount)}</span>   
      142 +            </div>                                            
      143 +          ))}                                                 
      144 +        </div>                                                
      145 +      </div>                                                  
      146      </div>                                                    
      147    )                                                           
      148  }                                                             
      149 +                                                              
      150 +function StatCard({ label, value, icon, color }: { label:     
          +string; value: string; icon: string; color: string }) {       
      151 +  return (                                                    
      152 +    <div className="rounded-xl border                         
          +border-[var(--border-subtle)] bg-[var(--bg-card)] p-5">       
      153 +      <div className="flex items-center gap-3">               
      154 +        <div className="flex h-10 w-10 items-center           
          +justify-center rounded-lg" style={{ backgroundColor:          
          +`${color}20` }}>                                              
      155 +          <span className="material-icons-outlined" style={{  
          +color, fontSize: '20px' }}>{icon}</span>                      
      156 +        </div>                                                
      157 +        <div>                                                 
      158 +          <p className="text-xs uppercase tracking-wide       
          +text-[var(--text-muted)]">{label}</p>                         
      159 +          <p className="text-2xl font-bold                    
          +text-[var(--text-primary)]">{value}</p>                       
      160 +        </div>                                                
      161 +      </div>                                                  
      162 +    </div>                                                    
      163 +  )                                                           
      164 +}                                                             
      165 +                                                              
      166 +function BarRow({ label, value, pct, color }: { label:        
          +string; value: string; pct: number; color: string }) {        
      167 +  return (                                                    
      168 +    <div>                                                     
      169 +      <div className="flex items-center justify-between       
          +text-sm">                                                     
      170 +        <span className="truncate                             
          +text-[var(--text-secondary)]">{label}</span>                  
      171 +        <span className="ml-2 font-medium                     
          +text-[var(--text-primary)]">{value}</span>                    
      172 +      </div>                                                  
      173 +      <div className="mt-1 h-1.5 w-full overflow-hidden       
          +rounded-full bg-[var(--bg-surface)]">                         
      174 +        <div className="h-full rounded-full transition-all"   
          +style={{ width: `${Math.max(2, pct * 100)}%`,                 
          +backgroundColor: color }} />                                  
      175 +      </div>                                                  
      176 +    </div>                                                    
      177 +  )                                                           
      178 +}

  - RAPID_CORE, RAPID_IMPORT, RAPID_FLOW, RAPID_COMMS, RAPID_API, CAM, DEX, C3,
  ATLAS

  ---
  The Bottom Line

  You went from a platform your team couldn't use (30-60 second loads, sandboxed
   iframes, 6-step deploys) to one that's instant, production-deployed, and 
  auto-deploying on every push. Same data, same business logic, completely
  different experience.

  toMachina is The Machine. It's real. It's live. And it's fast as fuck.
